## endstone [#endstone]

**Modules:**

- [**actor**](#endstone.actor) –
- [**ban**](#endstone.ban) –

- [**boss**](#endstone.boss) –

- [**map**](#endstone.map) –

- [**scheduler**](#endstone.scheduler) –
- [**scoreboard**](#endstone.scoreboard) –
- [**util**](#endstone.util) –

**Classes:**

- [**ColorFormat**](#endstone.ColorFormat) – All supported color and format codes.
- [**EnchantmentRegistry**](#endstone.EnchantmentRegistry) –
- [**GameMode**](#endstone.GameMode) – Represents the various type of game modes that Players may have.
- [**ItemRegistry**](#endstone.ItemRegistry) –
- [**Logger**](#endstone.Logger) – Logger class which can format and output varies levels of logs.
- [**NamespacedKey**](#endstone.NamespacedKey) – Represents a string-based key which consists of two components - a namespace and a key.
- [**OfflinePlayer**](#endstone.OfflinePlayer) – Represents a reference to a player identity and the data belonging to a player that is stored on the disk and can, thus, be retrieved without the player needing to be online.
- [**Player**](#endstone.Player) – Represents a player.
- [**Server**](#endstone.Server) – Represents a server implementation.
- [**Skin**](#endstone.Skin) – Represents a player skin.

### Logger [#endstone.Logger]

Logger class which can format and output varies levels of logs.

**Classes:**

- [**Level**](#endstone.Logger.Level) – Specifies the log level.

**Methods:**

- [**critical**](#endstone.Logger.critical) – Log a message at the CRITICAL level.
- [**debug**](#endstone.Logger.debug) – Log a message at the DEBUG level.
- [**error**](#endstone.Logger.error) – Log a message at the ERROR level.
- [**info**](#endstone.Logger.info) – Log a message at the INFO level.
- [**is_enabled_for**](#endstone.Logger.is_enabled_for) – Check if the Logger instance is enabled for the given log Level.
- [**set_level**](#endstone.Logger.set_level) – Set the logging level for this Logger instance.
- [**trace**](#endstone.Logger.trace) – Log a message at the TRACE level.
- [**warning**](#endstone.Logger.warning) – Log a message at the WARNING level.

**Attributes:**

- [**CRITICAL**](#endstone.Logger.CRITICAL) (<code>[Level](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Logger.Level)</code>) –
- [**DEBUG**](#endstone.Logger.DEBUG) (<code>[Level](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Logger.Level)</code>) –
- [**ERROR**](#endstone.Logger.ERROR) (<code>[Level](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Logger.Level)</code>) –
- [**INFO**](#endstone.Logger.INFO) (<code>[Level](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Logger.Level)</code>) –
- [**TRACE**](#endstone.Logger.TRACE) (<code>[Level](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Logger.Level)</code>) –
- [**WARNING**](#endstone.Logger.WARNING) (<code>[Level](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Logger.Level)</code>) –
- [**name**](#endstone.Logger.name) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Get the name of this Logger instance.

#### CRITICAL [#endstone.Logger.CRITICAL]

```python
CRITICAL: Logger.Level
```

#### DEBUG [#endstone.Logger.DEBUG]

```python
DEBUG: Logger.Level
```

#### ERROR [#endstone.Logger.ERROR]

```python
ERROR: Logger.Level
```

#### INFO [#endstone.Logger.INFO]

```python
INFO: Logger.Level
```

### NamespacedKey [#endstone.NamespacedKey]

```python
NamespacedKey(arg0:Plugin, arg1:str) -> None
```

Represents a string-based key which consists of two components - a namespace and a key.

**Methods:**

- [**from_string**](#endstone.NamespacedKey.from_string) – Parses a NamespacedKey from a string.

**Attributes:**

- [**key**](#endstone.NamespacedKey.key) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Returns the key of the NamespacedKey.
- [**namespace**](#endstone.NamespacedKey.namespace) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Returns the namespace of the NamespacedKey.

#### from_string [#endstone.NamespacedKey.from_string]

```python
from_string(input:str, plugin:Plugin = None) -> NamespacedKey
```

Parses a NamespacedKey from a string.

#### key [#endstone.NamespacedKey.key]

```python
key: str
```

Returns the key of the NamespacedKey.

#### namespace [#endstone.NamespacedKey.namespace]

```python
namespace: str
```

Returns the namespace of the NamespacedKey.

### OfflinePlayer [#endstone.OfflinePlayer]

Represents a reference to a player identity and the data belonging to a player that is stored on the disk and can, thus, be retrieved without the player needing to be online.

**Attributes:**

- [**name**](#endstone.OfflinePlayer.name) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Returns the name of this player
- [**unique_id**](#endstone.OfflinePlayer.unique_id) (<code>[UUID](#uuid.UUID)</code>) – Returns the UUID of this player

#### name [#endstone.OfflinePlayer.name]

```python
name: str
```

Returns the name of this player

#### unique_id [#endstone.OfflinePlayer.unique_id]

```python
unique_id: uuid.UUID
```

Returns the UUID of this player

### Player [#endstone.Player]

Bases: <code>[Mob](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Mob)</code>, <code>[OfflinePlayer](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.OfflinePlayer)</code>

Represents a player.

**Methods:**

- [**add_scoreboard_tag**](#endstone.Player.add_scoreboard_tag) – Adds a tag to this actor.
- [**close_form**](#endstone.Player.close_form) – Closes the forms that are currently open for the player.
- [**give_exp**](#endstone.Player.give_exp) – Gives the player the amount of experience specified.
- [**give_exp_levels**](#endstone.Player.give_exp_levels) – Gives the player the amount of experience levels specified.
- [**kick**](#endstone.Player.kick) – Kicks player with custom kick message.
- [**perform_command**](#endstone.Player.perform_command) – Makes the player perform the given command.
- [**play_sound**](#endstone.Player.play_sound) – Play a sound for a player at the location.
- [**recalculate_permissions**](#endstone.Player.recalculate_permissions) – Recalculates the permissions.
- [**remove**](#endstone.Player.remove) – Remove this actor from the level.
- [**remove_attachment**](#endstone.Player.remove_attachment) – Removes a given PermissionAttachment.
- [**remove_scoreboard_tag**](#endstone.Player.remove_scoreboard_tag) – Removes a given tag from this actor.
- [**reset_title**](#endstone.Player.reset_title) – Resets the title displayed to the player. This will clear the displayed title / subtitle and reset timings to their default values.
- [**send_error_message**](#endstone.Player.send_error_message) – Sends this sender an error message
- [**send_form**](#endstone.Player.send_form) – Sends a form to the player.
- [**send_message**](#endstone.Player.send_message) – Sends this sender a message
- [**send_packet**](#endstone.Player.send_packet) – Sends a packet to the player.
- [**send_popup**](#endstone.Player.send_popup) – Sends this player a popup message
- [**send_tip**](#endstone.Player.send_tip) – Sends this player a tip message
- [**send_title**](#endstone.Player.send_title) – Sends a title and a subtitle message to the player. If they are empty strings, the display will be updated as such.
- [**send_toast**](#endstone.Player.send_toast) – Sends this player a toast notification.
- [**set_rotation**](#endstone.Player.set_rotation) – Sets the actor's rotation.
- [**stop_all_sounds**](#endstone.Player.stop_all_sounds) – Stop all sounds from playing.
- [**stop_sound**](#endstone.Player.stop_sound) – Stop the specified sound from playing.
- [**transfer**](#endstone.Player.transfer) – Transfers the player to another server.
- [**update_commands**](#endstone.Player.update_commands) – Send the list of commands to the client.

**Attributes:**

- [**address**](#endstone.Player.address) (<code>[SocketAddress](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.SocketAddress)</code>) – Gets the socket address of this player
- [**allow_flight**](#endstone.Player.allow_flight) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – If the Player is allowed to fly via jump key double-tap.
- [**device_id**](#endstone.Player.device_id) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Get the player's current device id.
- [**device_os**](#endstone.Player.device_os) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Get the player's current device's operation system (OS).
- [**dimension**](#endstone.Player.dimension) (<code>[Dimension](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Dimension)</code>) – Gets the current Dimension this actor resides in.
- [**effective_permissions**](#endstone.Player.effective_permissions) (<code>[set](#set)\[[PermissionAttachmentInfo](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.PermissionAttachmentInfo)\]</code>) – Gets effective permissions.
- [**ender_chest**](#endstone.Player.ender_chest) (<code>[Inventory](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Inventory)</code>) – Get the player's EnderChest inventory.
- [**exp_level**](#endstone.Player.exp_level) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Gets or sets the players current experience level.
- [**exp_progress**](#endstone.Player.exp_progress) (<code>[float](#float)</code>) – Gets or sets the players current experience progress towards the next level.
- [**fly_speed**](#endstone.Player.fly_speed) (<code>[float](#float)</code>) – Gets or sets the current allowed speed that a client can fly.
- [**game_mode**](#endstone.Player.game_mode) (<code>[GameMode](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.GameMode)</code>) – The player's current game mode.
- [**game_version**](#endstone.Player.game_version) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Get the player's current game version.
- [**health**](#endstone.Player.health) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Gets or sets the entity's health from 0 to its max possible value, where 0 is dead.
- [**id**](#endstone.Player.id) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Returns a unique id for this actor.
- [**inventory**](#endstone.Player.inventory) (<code>[PlayerInventory](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.PlayerInventory)</code>) – Get the player's inventory.
- [**is_dead**](#endstone.Player.is_dead) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if this actor has been marked for removal.
- [**is_flying**](#endstone.Player.is_flying) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – If the player is currently flying or not.
- [**is_gliding**](#endstone.Player.is_gliding) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Checks to see if an actor is gliding, such as using an Elytra.
- [**is_in_lava**](#endstone.Player.is_in_lava) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if the actor is in lava.
- [**is_in_water**](#endstone.Player.is_in_water) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if the actor is in water.
- [**is_name_tag_always_visible**](#endstone.Player.is_name_tag_always_visible) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Gets or sets if the actor's name tag is always visible or not.
- [**is_name_tag_visible**](#endstone.Player.is_name_tag_visible) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Gets or sets if the actor's name tag is visible or not.
- [**is_on_ground**](#endstone.Player.is_on_ground) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if the actor is supported by a block, i.e. on ground.
- [**is_op**](#endstone.Player.is_op) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – The operator status of this playerall
- [**is_sneaking**](#endstone.Player.is_sneaking) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Gets or sets the sneak mode of the player
- [**is_sprinting**](#endstone.Player.is_sprinting) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Gets or sets whether the player is sprinting or not.
- [**is_valid**](#endstone.Player.is_valid) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns false if the entity has died, been despawned for some other reason, or has not been added to the level.
- [**level**](#endstone.Player.level) (<code>[Level](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Level)</code>) – Gets the current Level this actor resides in.
- [**locale**](#endstone.Player.locale) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Get the player's current locale.
- [**location**](#endstone.Player.location) (<code>[Location](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Location)</code>) – Gets the actor's current position.
- [**max_health**](#endstone.Player.max_health) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Gets the maximum health this entity has.
- [**name**](#endstone.Player.name) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Returns the name of this player
- [**name_tag**](#endstone.Player.name_tag) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gets or sets the current name tag of the actor.
- [**permission_level**](#endstone.Player.permission_level) (<code>[PermissionLevel](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.PermissionLevel)</code>) – Gets the permission level of this object
- [**ping**](#endstone.Player.ping) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Gets the player's average ping in milliseconds.
- [**runtime_id**](#endstone.Player.runtime_id) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Returns the runtime id for this actor.
- [**score_tag**](#endstone.Player.score_tag) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gets or sets the current score tag of the actor.
- [**scoreboard**](#endstone.Player.scoreboard) (<code>[Scoreboard](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Scoreboard)</code>) – Gets or sets the player's visible Scoreboard.
- [**scoreboard_tags**](#endstone.Player.scoreboard_tags) (<code>[list](#list)\[[str](#str)\]</code>) – Returns a list of scoreboard tags for this actor.
- [**server**](#endstone.Player.server) (<code>[Server](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Server)</code>) – Returns the server instance that this command is running on
- [**skin**](#endstone.Player.skin) (<code>[Skin](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Skin)</code>) – Get the player's skin.
- [**total_exp**](#endstone.Player.total_exp) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Gets the players total experience points.
- [**type**](#endstone.Player.type) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gets the type of the actor.
- [**unique_id**](#endstone.Player.unique_id) (<code>[UUID](#uuid.UUID)</code>) – Returns the UUID of this player
- [**velocity**](#endstone.Player.velocity) (<code>[Vector](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Vector)</code>) – Gets this actor's current velocity.
- [**walk_speed**](#endstone.Player.walk_speed) (<code>[float](#float)</code>) – Gets or sets the current allowed speed that a client can walk.
- [**xuid**](#endstone.Player.xuid) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Returns the Xbox User ID (XUID) of this player

### Server [#endstone.Server]

Represents a server implementation.

**Methods:**

- [**broadcast**](#endstone.Server.broadcast) – Broadcasts the specified message to every user with the given permission name.
- [**broadcast_message**](#endstone.Server.broadcast_message) – Broadcasts the specified message to every user with permission endstone.broadcast.user
- [**create_block_data**](#endstone.Server.create_block_data) – Creates a new BlockData instance for the specified block type, with all properties initialized to defaults, except for those provided.
- [**create_boss_bar**](#endstone.Server.create_boss_bar) – Creates a boss bar instance to display to players. The progress defaults to 1.0.
- [**create_scoreboard**](#endstone.Server.create_scoreboard) – Creates a new Scoreboard to be tracked by the server.
- [**dispatch_command**](#endstone.Server.dispatch_command) – Dispatches a command on this server, and executes it if found.
- [**get_plugin_command**](#endstone.Server.get_plugin_command) – Gets a PluginCommand with the given name or alias.
- [**reload**](#endstone.Server.reload) – Reloads the server configuration, functions, scripts and plugins.
- [**reload_data**](#endstone.Server.reload_data) – Reload only the Minecraft data for the server.
- [**shutdown**](#endstone.Server.shutdown) – Shutdowns the server, stopping everything.

**Attributes:**

- [**average_mspt**](#endstone.Server.average_mspt) (<code>[float](#float)</code>) – Gets the average milliseconds per tick (MSPT).
- [**average_tick_usage**](#endstone.Server.average_tick_usage) (<code>[float](#float)</code>) – Gets the average tick usage of the server.
- [**average_tps**](#endstone.Server.average_tps) (<code>[float](#float)</code>) – Gets the average ticks per second (TPS).
- [**ban_list**](#endstone.Server.ban_list) (<code>[PlayerBanList](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.PlayerBanList)</code>) – Gets the player ban list.
- [**command_sender**](#endstone.Server.command_sender) (<code>[ConsoleCommandSender](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.ConsoleCommandSender)</code>) – Gets a CommandSender for this server.
- [**current_mspt**](#endstone.Server.current_mspt) (<code>[float](#float)</code>) – Gets the current milliseconds per tick (MSPT).
- [**current_tick_usage**](#endstone.Server.current_tick_usage) (<code>[float](#float)</code>) – Gets the current tick usage of the server.
- [**current_tps**](#endstone.Server.current_tps) (<code>[float](#float)</code>) – Gets the current ticks per second (TPS).
- [**enchantment_registry**](#endstone.Server.enchantment_registry) (<code>[EnchantmentRegistry](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.EnchantmentRegistry)</code>) – Returns the registry for all the enchantments.
- [**ip_ban_list**](#endstone.Server.ip_ban_list) (<code>[IpBanList](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.IpBanList)</code>) – Gets the IP ban list.
- [**item_factory**](#endstone.Server.item_factory) (<code>[ItemFactory](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.ItemFactory)</code>) – Gets the instance of the item factory (for ItemMeta).
- [**item_registry**](#endstone.Server.item_registry) (<code>[ItemRegistry](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.ItemRegistry)</code>) – Returns the registry for all the item types.
- [**language**](#endstone.Server.language) (<code>[Language](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Language)</code>) – Gets the current language interface used by the server.
- [**level**](#endstone.Server.level) (<code>[Level](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Level)</code>) – Gets the server level.
- [**logger**](#endstone.Server.logger) (<code>[Logger](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Logger)</code>) – Returns the primary logger associated with this server instance.
- [**max_players**](#endstone.Server.max_players) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – The maximum amount of players which can login to this server.
- [**minecraft_version**](#endstone.Server.minecraft_version) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gets the Minecraft version that this server is running.
- [**name**](#endstone.Server.name) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gets the name of this server implementation.
- [**online_mode**](#endstone.Server.online_mode) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Gets whether the Server is in online mode or not.
- [**online_players**](#endstone.Server.online_players) (<code>[list](#list)\[[Player](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Player)\]</code>) – Gets a list of all currently online players.
- [**plugin_manager**](#endstone.Server.plugin_manager) (<code>[PluginManager](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.PluginManager)</code>) – Gets the plugin manager for interfacing with plugins.
- [**port**](#endstone.Server.port) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Get the game port that the server runs on.
- [**port_v6**](#endstone.Server.port_v6) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Get the game port (IPv6) that the server runs on.
- [**protocol_version**](#endstone.Server.protocol_version) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Gets the network protocol version that this server supports.
- [**scheduler**](#endstone.Server.scheduler) (<code>[Scheduler](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Scheduler)</code>) – Gets the scheduler for managing scheduled events.
- [**scoreboard**](#endstone.Server.scoreboard) (<code>[Scoreboard](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Scoreboard)</code>) – Gets the primary Scoreboard controlled by the server.
- [**service_manager**](#endstone.Server.service_manager) (<code>[ServiceManager](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.ServiceManager)</code>) – Gets the service manager.
- [**start_time**](#endstone.Server.start_time) (<code>[datetime](#datetime.datetime)</code>) – Gets the start time of the server.
- [**version**](#endstone.Server.version) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gets the version of this server implementation.

### actor [#actor]

**Classes:**

- [**Actor**](#endstone.actor.Actor) – Represents a base actor in the level.
- [**Item**](#endstone.actor.Item) – Represents a base actor in the level.
- [**Mob**](#endstone.actor.Mob) – Represents a mobile entity (i.e. living entity), such as a monster or player.

#### Actor [#endstone.actor.Actor]

Bases: <code>[CommandSender](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.CommandSender)</code>

Represents a base actor in the level.

**Methods:**

- [**add_scoreboard_tag**](#endstone.actor.Actor.add_scoreboard_tag) – Adds a tag to this actor.
- [**recalculate_permissions**](#endstone.actor.Actor.recalculate_permissions) – Recalculates the permissions.
- [**remove**](#endstone.actor.Actor.remove) – Remove this actor from the level.
- [**remove_attachment**](#endstone.actor.Actor.remove_attachment) – Removes a given PermissionAttachment.
- [**remove_scoreboard_tag**](#endstone.actor.Actor.remove_scoreboard_tag) – Removes a given tag from this actor.
- [**send_error_message**](#endstone.actor.Actor.send_error_message) – Sends this sender an error message
- [**send_message**](#endstone.actor.Actor.send_message) – Sends this sender a message
- [**set_rotation**](#endstone.actor.Actor.set_rotation) – Sets the actor's rotation.

**Attributes:**

- [**dimension**](#endstone.actor.Actor.dimension) (<code>[Dimension](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Dimension)</code>) – Gets the current Dimension this actor resides in.
- [**effective_permissions**](#endstone.actor.Actor.effective_permissions) (<code>[set](#set)\[[PermissionAttachmentInfo](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.PermissionAttachmentInfo)\]</code>) – Gets effective permissions.
- [**health**](#endstone.actor.Actor.health) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Gets or sets the entity's health from 0 to its max possible value, where 0 is dead.
- [**id**](#endstone.actor.Actor.id) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Returns a unique id for this actor.
- [**is_dead**](#endstone.actor.Actor.is_dead) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if this actor has been marked for removal.
- [**is_in_lava**](#endstone.actor.Actor.is_in_lava) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if the actor is in lava.
- [**is_in_water**](#endstone.actor.Actor.is_in_water) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if the actor is in water.
- [**is_name_tag_always_visible**](#endstone.actor.Actor.is_name_tag_always_visible) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Gets or sets if the actor's name tag is always visible or not.
- [**is_name_tag_visible**](#endstone.actor.Actor.is_name_tag_visible) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Gets or sets if the actor's name tag is visible or not.
- [**is_on_ground**](#endstone.actor.Actor.is_on_ground) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if the actor is supported by a block, i.e. on ground.
- [**is_valid**](#endstone.actor.Actor.is_valid) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns false if the entity has died, been despawned for some other reason, or has not been added to the level.
- [**level**](#endstone.actor.Actor.level) (<code>[Level](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Level)</code>) – Gets the current Level this actor resides in.

#### Item [#endstone.actor.Item]

Bases: <code>[Actor](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Actor)</code>

Represents a base actor in the level.

**Methods:**

- [**add_scoreboard_tag**](#endstone.actor.Item.add_scoreboard_tag) – Adds a tag to this actor.
- [**recalculate_permissions**](#endstone.actor.Item.recalculate_permissions) – Recalculates the permissions.
- [**remove**](#endstone.actor.Item.remove) – Remove this actor from the level.
- [**remove_attachment**](#endstone.actor.Item.remove_attachment) – Removes a given PermissionAttachment.
- [**remove_scoreboard_tag**](#endstone.actor.Item.remove_scoreboard_tag) – Removes a given tag from this actor.
- [**send_error_message**](#endstone.actor.Item.send_error_message) – Sends this sender an error message
- [**send_message**](#endstone.actor.Item.send_message) – Sends this sender a message
- [**set_rotation**](#endstone.actor.Item.set_rotation) – Sets the actor's rotation.

**Attributes:**

- [**dimension**](#endstone.actor.Item.dimension) (<code>[Dimension](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Dimension)</code>) – Gets the current Dimension this actor resides in.
- [**effective_permissions**](#endstone.actor.Item.effective_permissions) (<code>[set](#set)\[[PermissionAttachmentInfo](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.PermissionAttachmentInfo)\]</code>) – Gets effective permissions.
- [**health**](#endstone.actor.Item.health) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Gets or sets the entity's health from 0 to its max possible value, where 0 is dead.
- [**id**](#endstone.actor.Item.id) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Returns a unique id for this actor.
- [**is_dead**](#endstone.actor.Item.is_dead) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if this actor has been marked for removal.
- [**is_in_lava**](#endstone.actor.Item.is_in_lava) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if the actor is in lava.
- [**is_in_water**](#endstone.actor.Item.is_in_water) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if the actor is in water.
- [**is_name_tag_always_visible**](#endstone.actor.Item.is_name_tag_always_visible) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Gets or sets if the actor's name tag is always visible or not.
- [**is_name_tag_visible**](#endstone.actor.Item.is_name_tag_visible) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Gets or sets if the actor's name tag is visible or not.
- [**is_on_ground**](#endstone.actor.Item.is_on_ground) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if the actor is supported by a block, i.e. on ground.
- [**is_unlimited_lifetime**](#endstone.actor.Item.is_unlimited_lifetime) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Gets or sets if this Item lives forever
- [**is_valid**](#endstone.actor.Item.is_valid) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns false if the entity has died, been despawned for some other reason, or has not been added to the level.
- [**item_stack**](#endstone.actor.Item.item_stack) (<code>[ItemStack](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.ItemStack)</code>) – Gets or sets the item stack associated with this item drop.
- [**level**](#endstone.actor.Item.level) (<code>[Level](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Level)</code>) – Gets the current Level this actor resides in.
- [**location**](#endstone.actor.Item.location) (<code>[Location](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Location)</code>) – Gets the actor's current position.
- [**max_health**](#endstone.actor.Item.max_health) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Gets the maximum health this entity has.
- [**name**](#endstone.actor.Item.name) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gets the name of this command sender
- [**name_tag**](#endstone.actor.Item.name_tag) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gets or sets the current name tag of the actor.
- [**permission_level**](#endstone.actor.Item.permission_level) (<code>[PermissionLevel](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.PermissionLevel)</code>) – Gets the permission level of this object
- [**pickup_delay**](#endstone.actor.Item.pickup_delay) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Gets or sets the delay before this Item is available to be picked up by players.
- [**runtime_id**](#endstone.actor.Item.runtime_id) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Returns the runtime id for this actor.
- [**score_tag**](#endstone.actor.Item.score_tag) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gets or sets the current score tag of the actor.
- [**scoreboard_tags**](#endstone.actor.Item.scoreboard_tags) (<code>[list](#list)\[[str](#str)\]</code>) – Returns a list of scoreboard tags for this actor.
- [**server**](#endstone.actor.Item.server) (<code>[Server](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Server)</code>) – Returns the server instance that this command is running on
- [**thrower**](#endstone.actor.Item.thrower) (<code>[int](#int) | None</code>) – Gets or sets the thrower of this item.
- [**type**](#endstone.actor.Item.type) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gets the type of the actor.
- [**velocity**](#endstone.actor.Item.velocity) (<code>[Vector](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Vector)</code>) – Gets this actor's current velocity.

#### Mob [#endstone.actor.Mob]

Bases: <code>[Actor](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Actor)</code>

Represents a mobile entity (i.e. living entity), such as a monster or player.

**Methods:**

- [**add_scoreboard_tag**](#endstone.actor.Mob.add_scoreboard_tag) – Adds a tag to this actor.
- [**recalculate_permissions**](#endstone.actor.Mob.recalculate_permissions) – Recalculates the permissions.
- [**remove**](#endstone.actor.Mob.remove) – Remove this actor from the level.
- [**remove_attachment**](#endstone.actor.Mob.remove_attachment) – Removes a given PermissionAttachment.
- [**remove_scoreboard_tag**](#endstone.actor.Mob.remove_scoreboard_tag) – Removes a given tag from this actor.
- [**send_error_message**](#endstone.actor.Mob.send_error_message) – Sends this sender an error message
- [**send_message**](#endstone.actor.Mob.send_message) – Sends this sender a message
- [**set_rotation**](#endstone.actor.Mob.set_rotation) – Sets the actor's rotation.

**Attributes:**

- [**dimension**](#endstone.actor.Mob.dimension) (<code>[Dimension](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Dimension)</code>) – Gets the current Dimension this actor resides in.
- [**effective_permissions**](#endstone.actor.Mob.effective_permissions) (<code>[set](#set)\[[PermissionAttachmentInfo](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.PermissionAttachmentInfo)\]</code>) – Gets effective permissions.
- [**health**](#endstone.actor.Mob.health) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Gets or sets the entity's health from 0 to its max possible value, where 0 is dead.
- [**id**](#endstone.actor.Mob.id) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Returns a unique id for this actor.
- [**is_dead**](#endstone.actor.Mob.is_dead) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if this actor has been marked for removal.
- [**is_gliding**](#endstone.actor.Mob.is_gliding) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Checks to see if an actor is gliding, such as using an Elytra.
- [**is_in_lava**](#endstone.actor.Mob.is_in_lava) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if the actor is in lava.
- [**is_in_water**](#endstone.actor.Mob.is_in_water) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if the actor is in water.
- [**is_name_tag_always_visible**](#endstone.actor.Mob.is_name_tag_always_visible) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Gets or sets if the actor's name tag is always visible or not.
- [**is_name_tag_visible**](#endstone.actor.Mob.is_name_tag_visible) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Gets or sets if the actor's name tag is visible or not.
- [**is_on_ground**](#endstone.actor.Mob.is_on_ground) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if the actor is supported by a block, i.e. on ground.
- [**is_valid**](#endstone.actor.Mob.is_valid) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns false if the entity has died, been despawned for some other reason, or has not been added to the level.

- [**location**](#endstone.actor.Mob.location) (<code>[Location](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Location)</code>) – Gets the actor's current position.
- [**max_health**](#endstone.actor.Mob.max_health) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Gets the maximum health this entity has.
- [**name**](#endstone.actor.Mob.name) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gets the name of this command sender
- [**name_tag**](#endstone.actor.Mob.name_tag) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gets or sets the current name tag of the actor.
- [**permission_level**](#endstone.actor.Mob.permission_level) (<code>[PermissionLevel](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.PermissionLevel)</code>) – Gets the permission level of this object
- [**runtime_id**](#endstone.actor.Mob.runtime_id) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Returns the runtime id for this actor.
- [**score_tag**](#endstone.actor.Mob.score_tag) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gets or sets the current score tag of the actor.

#### Block [#endstone.block.Block]

Represents a block.

**Methods:**

- [**capture_state**](#endstone.block.Block.capture_state) – Captures the current state of this block. The returned object will never be updated, and you are not guaranteed that (for example) a sign is still a sign after you capture its state.
- [**set_data**](#endstone.block.Block.set_data) – Sets the complete data for this block
- [**set_type**](#endstone.block.Block.set_type) – Sets the type of this block

**Attributes:**

#### BossBar [#endstone.boss.BossBar]

Represents a boss bar that is displayed to players.

**Methods:**

- [**add_flag**](#endstone.boss.BossBar.add_flag) – Adds an optional flag to this boss bar.
- [**add_player**](#endstone.boss.BossBar.add_player) – Adds the player to this boss bar causing it to display on their screen.
- [**has_flag**](#endstone.boss.BossBar.has_flag) – Checks whether this boss bar has the passed flag set.
- [**remove_all**](#endstone.boss.BossBar.remove_all) – Removes all players from this boss bar.
- [**remove_flag**](#endstone.boss.BossBar.remove_flag) – Removes an existing flag on this boss bar.
- [**remove_player**](#endstone.boss.BossBar.remove_player) – Removes the player from this boss bar causing it to be removed from their screen.

**Attributes:**

- [**color**](#endstone.boss.BossBar.color) (<code>[BarColor](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.BarColor)</code>) – The color of this boss bar.
- [**is_visible**](#endstone.boss.BossBar.is_visible) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – If the boss bar is displayed to attached players.
- [**players**](#endstone.boss.BossBar.players) (<code>[list](#list)\[[Player](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Player)\]</code>) – Returns all players viewing this boss bar.
- [**progress**](#endstone.boss.BossBar.progress) (<code>[float](#float)</code>) – The progress of the bar between 0.0 and 1.0.
- [**style**](#endstone.boss.BossBar.style) (<code>[BarStyle](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.BarStyle)</code>) – The style of this boss bar.
- [**title**](#endstone.boss.BossBar.title) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – The title of this boss bar.

### command [#command]

**Classes:**

- [**BlockCommandSender**](#endstone.command.BlockCommandSender) – Represents a block command sender.
- [**Command**](#endstone.command.Command) – Represents a Command, which executes various tasks upon user input
- [**CommandExecutor**](#endstone.command.CommandExecutor) – Represents a class which contains a single method for executing commands
- [**CommandSender**](#endstone.command.CommandSender) – Represents a command sender.
- [**CommandSenderWrapper**](#endstone.command.CommandSenderWrapper) – Represents a wrapper that forwards commands to the wrapped CommandSender and captures its output
- [**ConsoleCommandSender**](#endstone.command.ConsoleCommandSender) – Represents a console command sender.

#### Command [#endstone.command.Command]

```python
Command(
    name: str,
    description: str | None = None,
    usages: list[str] | None = None,
    aliases: list[str] | None = None,
    permissions: list[str] | None = None,
    *args: list[str] | None,
    **kwargs: list[str] | None
) -> None
```

Represents a Command, which executes various tasks upon user input

**Methods:**

- [**execute**](#endstone.command.Command.execute) – Executes the command, returning its success
- [**test_permission**](#endstone.command.Command.test_permission) – Tests the given CommandSender to see if they can perform this command.
- [**test_permission_silently**](#endstone.command.Command.test_permission_silently) – Tests the given CommandSender to see if they can perform this command. No error is sent to the sender.

**Attributes:**

- [**aliases**](#endstone.command.Command.aliases) (<code>[list](#list)\[[str](#str)\]</code>) – List of aliases of this command
- [**description**](#endstone.command.Command.description) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Brief description of this command
- [**is_registered**](#endstone.command.Command.is_registered) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns the current registered state of this command
- [**name**](#endstone.command.Command.name) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Name of this command.
- [**permissions**](#endstone.command.Command.permissions) (<code>[list](#list)\[[str](#str)\]</code>) – The permissions required by users to be able to perform this command
- [**usages**](#endstone.command.Command.usages) (<code>[list](#list)\[[str](#str)\]</code>) – List of usages of this command

##### aliases [#endstone.command.Command.aliases]

```python
aliases: list[str]
```

List of aliases of this command

##### description [#endstone.command.Command.description]

```python
description: str
```

Brief description of this command

##### execute [#endstone.command.Command.execute]

```python
execute(sender:CommandSender, args:list[str]) -> bool
```

Executes the command, returning its success

##### is_registered [#endstone.command.Command.is_registered]

```python
is_registered: bool
```

Returns the current registered state of this command

##### name [#endstone.command.Command.name]

```python
name: str
```

Name of this command.

##### permissions [#endstone.command.Command.permissions]

```python
permissions: list[str]
```

The permissions required by users to be able to perform this command

##### test_permission [#endstone.command.Command.test_permission]

```python
test_permission(target:CommandSender) -> bool
```

Tests the given CommandSender to see if they can perform this command.

##### test_permission_silently [#endstone.command.Command.test_permission_silently]

```python
test_permission_silently(target:CommandSender) -> bool
```

Tests the given CommandSender to see if they can perform this command. No error is sent to the sender.


List of usages of this command

### event [#event]

**Classes:**

- [**ActorDamageEvent**](#endstone.event.ActorDamageEvent) – Called when an Actor is damaged.
- [**ActorDeathEvent**](#endstone.event.ActorDeathEvent) – Called when an Actor dies.
- [**ActorEvent**](#endstone.event.ActorEvent) – Represents an Actor-related event.
- [**ActorExplodeEvent**](#endstone.event.ActorExplodeEvent) – Called when an Actor explodes.
- [**ActorKnockbackEvent**](#endstone.event.ActorKnockbackEvent) – Called when a living entity receives knockback.
- [**ActorRemoveEvent**](#endstone.event.ActorRemoveEvent) – Called when an Actor is removed.
- [**ActorSpawnEvent**](#endstone.event.ActorSpawnEvent) – Called when an Actor is spawned into a world.
- [**ActorTeleportEvent**](#endstone.event.ActorTeleportEvent) – Called when a non-player entity is teleported from one location to another.
- [**BlockBreakEvent**](#endstone.event.BlockBreakEvent) – Called when a block is broken by a player.
- [**BlockCookEvent**](#endstone.event.BlockCookEvent) – Called when an ItemStack is successfully cooked in a block.
- [**BlockEvent**](#endstone.event.BlockEvent) – Represents an Block-related event
- [**BlockPistonEvent**](#endstone.event.BlockPistonEvent) – Called when a piston block is triggered
- [**BlockPistonExtendEvent**](#endstone.event.BlockPistonExtendEvent) – Called when a piston extends.
- [**BlockPistonRetractEvent**](#endstone.event.BlockPistonRetractEvent) – Called when a piston retracts.
- [**BlockPlaceEvent**](#endstone.event.BlockPlaceEvent) – Called when a block is placed by a player.
- [**BroadcastMessageEvent**](#endstone.event.BroadcastMessageEvent) – Event triggered for server broadcast messages such as from Server.broadcast
- [**Cancellable**](#endstone.event.Cancellable) – Represents an event that may be cancelled by a plugin or the server.
- [**ChunkEvent**](#endstone.event.ChunkEvent) – Represents a Chunk related event
- [**ChunkLoadEvent**](#endstone.event.ChunkLoadEvent) – Called when a chunk is loaded
- [**ChunkUnloadEvent**](#endstone.event.ChunkUnloadEvent) – Called when a chunk is unloaded
- [**DimensionEvent**](#endstone.event.DimensionEvent) – Represents events within a dimension
- [**Event**](#endstone.event.Event) – Represents an event.
- [**EventPriority**](#endstone.event.EventPriority) – Listeners are called in following order: LOWEST -> LOW -> NORMAL -> HIGH -> HIGHEST -> MONITOR
- [**EventResult**](#endstone.event.EventResult) –
- [**LeavesDecayEvent**](#endstone.event.LeavesDecayEvent) – Called when leaves are decaying naturally.
- [**LevelEvent**](#endstone.event.LevelEvent) – Represents events within a level
- [**MobEvent**](#endstone.event.MobEvent) – Represents an Mob-related event.
- [**PacketReceiveEvent**](#endstone.event.PacketReceiveEvent) – Called when the server receives a packet from a connected client.
- [**PacketSendEvent**](#endstone.event.PacketSendEvent) – Called when the server sends a packet to a connected client.
- [**PlayerBedEnterEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerBedEnterEvent) – Called when a player is almost about to enter the bed.
- [**PlayerBedLeaveEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerBedLeaveEvent) – Called when a player is leaving a bed.
- [**PlayerChatEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerChatEvent) – Called when a player sends a chat message.
- [**PlayerCommandEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerCommandEvent) – Called whenever a player runs a command.
- [**PlayerDeathEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerDeathEvent) – Called when a player dies
- [**PlayerDropItemEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerDropItemEvent) – Called when a player drops an item from their inventory
- [**PlayerEmoteEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerEmoteEvent) – Called when a player uses and emote
- [**PlayerEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerEvent) – Represents a player related event
- [**PlayerGameModeChangeEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerGameModeChangeEvent) – Called when the GameMode of the player is changed.
- [**PlayerInteractActorEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerInteractActorEvent) – Represents an event that is called when a player right-clicks an actor.
- [**PlayerInteractEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerInteractEvent) – Represents an event that is called when a player right-clicks a block.
- [**PlayerItemConsumeEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerItemConsumeEvent) – Called when a player is finishing consuming an item (food, potion, milk bucket).
- [**PlayerItemHeldEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerItemHeldEvent) – Called when a player changes their currently held item.
- [**PlayerJoinEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerJoinEvent) – Called when a player joins a server
- [**PlayerJumpEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerJumpEvent) – Called when a player jumps.
- [**PlayerKickEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerKickEvent) – Called when a player gets kicked from the server
- [**PlayerLoginEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerLoginEvent) – Called when a player attempts to login in.
- [**PlayerMoveEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerMoveEvent) – Called when a player moves.
- [**PlayerPickupItemEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerPickupItemEvent) – Called when a player picks an item up from the ground.
- [**PlayerQuitEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerQuitEvent) – Called when a player leaves a server.
- [**PlayerRespawnEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerRespawnEvent) – Called when a player respawns.
- [**PlayerSkinChangeEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerSkinChangeEvent) – Called when a player changes their skin.
- [**PlayerTeleportEvent**](#endstone.event.PlayerTeleportEvent) – Called when a player is teleported from one location to another.
- [**PluginDisableEvent**](#endstone.event.PluginDisableEvent) – Called when a plugin is disabled.
- [**PluginEnableEvent**](#endstone.event.PluginEnableEvent) – Called when a plugin is enabled.
- [**ScriptMessageEvent**](#endstone.event.ScriptMessageEvent) – Called when a message is sent by `/scriptevent` command
- [**ServerCommandEvent**](#endstone.event.ServerCommandEvent) – Called when the console runs a command, early in the process.
- [**ServerEvent**](#endstone.event.ServerEvent) – Represents a server-related event
- [**ServerListPingEvent**](#endstone.event.ServerListPingEvent) – Called when a server ping is coming in.
- [**ServerLoadEvent**](#endstone.event.ServerLoadEvent) – Called when either the server startup or reload has completed.
- [**ThunderChangeEvent**](#endstone.event.ThunderChangeEvent) – Called when the thunder state in a world is changing.
- [**WeatherChangeEvent**](#endstone.event.WeatherChangeEvent) – Called when the weather (rain) state in a world is changing.
- [**WeatherEvent**](#endstone.event.WeatherEvent) – Represents a weather-related event

#### ActorDamageEvent [#endstone.event.ActorDamageEvent]

Bases: <code>[BlockEvent](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.BlockEvent)</code>, <code>[Cancellable](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Cancellable)</code>

#### PacketReceiveEvent [#endstone.event.PacketReceiveEvent]

Bases: <code>[ServerEvent](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.ServerEvent)</code>, <code>[Cancellable](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Cancellable)</code>

Called when the server receives a packet from a connected client.

- [**cancel**](#endstone.event.PacketReceiveEvent.cancel) – Cancel this event. A cancelled event will not be executed in the server, but will still pass to other plugins.

**Attributes:**

- [**address**](#endstone.event.PacketReceiveEvent.address) (<code>[SocketAddress](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.SocketAddress)</code>) – Gets the network address to which this packet is being sent.

- [**packet_id**](#endstone.event.PacketReceiveEvent.packet_id) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Gets the ID of the packet.
- [**payload**](#endstone.event.PacketReceiveEvent.payload) (<code>[bytes](#bytes)</code>) – Gets or sets the raw packet data **excluding** the header.
- [**player**](#endstone.event.PacketReceiveEvent.player) (<code>[Player](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Player)</code>) – Gets the player involved in this event
- [**sub_client_id**](#endstone.event.PacketReceiveEvent.sub_client_id) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Gets the SubClient ID (0 = primary client; 1-3 = split-screen clients).

### form [#form]

**Classes:**

- [**ActionForm**](#endstone.form.ActionForm) – Represents a form with buttons that let the player take action.
- [**Button**](#endstone.form.Button) – Represents a button with text and an optional icon.
- [**Divider**](#endstone.form.Divider) – Represents a divider.
- [**Dropdown**](#endstone.form.Dropdown) – Represents a dropdown with a set of predefined options.
- [**Header**](#endstone.form.Header) – Represents a header with a label.
- [**Label**](#endstone.form.Label) – Represents a text label.
- [**MessageForm**](#endstone.form.MessageForm) – Represents a form with two buttons.
- [**ModalForm**](#endstone.form.ModalForm) – Represents a modal form with controls.
- [**Slider**](#endstone.form.Slider) – Represents a slider with a label.
- [**StepSlider**](#endstone.form.StepSlider) – Represents a step slider with a set of predefined options.
- [**TextInput**](#endstone.form.TextInput) – Represents a text input field.
- [**Toggle**](#endstone.form.Toggle) – Represents a toggle button with a label.

#### Inventory [#endstone.inventory.Inventory]

Interface to the various inventories.

**Methods:**

- [**add_item**](#endstone.inventory.Inventory.add_item) – Stores the given ItemStacks in the inventory.
- [**get_item**](#endstone.inventory.Inventory.get_item) – Returns the ItemStack found in the slot at the given index
- [**remove_item**](#endstone.inventory.Inventory.remove_item) – Removes the given ItemStacks from the inventory.
- [**set_item**](#endstone.inventory.Inventory.set_item) – Stores the ItemStack at the given index of the inventory.

**Attributes:**

- [**contents**](#endstone.inventory.Inventory.contents) (<code>[list](#list)\[[ItemStack](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.ItemStack)\]</code>) – Returns all ItemStacks from the inventory
- [**first_empty**](#endstone.inventory.Inventory.first_empty) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Returns the first empty Slot.
- [**is_empty**](#endstone.inventory.Inventory.is_empty) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Check whether this inventory is empty. An inventory is considered to be empty if there are no ItemStacks in any slot of this inventory.
- [**max_stack_size**](#endstone.inventory.Inventory.max_stack_size) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Returns the maximum stack size for an ItemStack in this inventory.
- [**size**](#endstone.inventory.Inventory.size) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Returns the size of the inventory

##### add_item [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.add_item]

```python
add_item(*args) -> dict[int, ItemStack]
```

Stores the given ItemStacks in the inventory.
This will try to fill existing stacks and empty slots as well as it can.

The returned map contains what it couldn't store, where the key is the index, and the value is the ItemStack.
If all items are stored, it will return an empty dict.

##### contents [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.contents]

```python
contents: list[ItemStack]
```

Returns all ItemStacks from the inventory

##### first_empty [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.first_empty]

```python
first_empty: int
```

Returns the first empty Slot.

##### get_item [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.get_item]

```python
get_item(index:int) -> ItemStack
```

Returns the ItemStack found in the slot at the given index

##### is_empty [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.is_empty]

```python
is_empty: bool
```

Check whether this inventory is empty. An inventory is considered to be empty if there are no ItemStacks in any slot of this inventory.

##### max_stack_size [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.max_stack_size]

```python
max_stack_size: int
```

Returns the maximum stack size for an ItemStack in this inventory.

##### remove_item [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.remove_item]

```python
remove_item(*args) -> dict[int, ItemStack]
```

Removes the given ItemStacks from the inventory.
It will try to remove 'as much as possible' from the types and amounts you give as arguments.

The returned HashMap contains what it couldn't remove, where the key is the index, and the value is the ItemStack.
If all the given ItemStacks are removed, it will return an empty dict.

##### set_item [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.set_item]

```python
set_item(index:int, item:ItemStack) -> None
```

Stores the ItemStack at the given index of the inventory.

##### size [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.size]

```python
size: int
```

Returns the size of the inventory

#### ItemFactory [#endstone.inventory.ItemFactory]

**Methods:**

- [**as_meta_for**](#endstone.inventory.ItemFactory.as_meta_for) – Returns an appropriate item meta for the specified item type.
- [**equals**](#endstone.inventory.ItemFactory.equals) – This method is used to compare two ItemMeta objects.
- [**get_item_meta**](#endstone.inventory.ItemFactory.get_item_meta) – This creates a new item meta for the item type.
- [**is_applicable**](#endstone.inventory.ItemFactory.is_applicable) – This method checks the item meta to confirm that it is applicable (no data lost if applied) to the specified ItemStack




#### ItemMeta [#endstone.inventory.ItemMeta]

Represents the metadata of a generic item.

**Methods:**

- [**add_enchant**](#endstone.inventory.ItemMeta.add_enchant) – Adds the specified enchantment to this item meta.
- [**clone**](#endstone.inventory.ItemMeta.clone) – Creates a clone of the current metadata.
- [**get_enchant_level**](#endstone.inventory.ItemMeta.get_enchant_level) – Checks for the level of the specified enchantment.
- [**has_enchant**](#endstone.inventory.ItemMeta.has_enchant) – Checks for existence of the specified enchantment.
- [**remove_enchant**](#endstone.inventory.ItemMeta.remove_enchant) – Removes the specified enchantment from this item meta.
- [**remove_enchants**](#endstone.inventory.ItemMeta.remove_enchants) – Removes all enchantments from this item meta.

**Attributes:**

- [**damage**](#endstone.inventory.ItemMeta.damage) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Gets or sets the damage.
- [**display_name**](#endstone.inventory.ItemMeta.display_name) (<code>[str](#str) | None</code>) – Gets or sets the display name.
- [**enchants**](#endstone.inventory.ItemMeta.enchants) (<code>[dict](#dict)\[[str](#str), [int](#int)\]</code>) – Returns a copy the enchantments in this ItemMeta.
- [**has_damage**](#endstone.inventory.ItemMeta.has_damage) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Checks to see if this item has damage.
- [**has_display_name**](#endstone.inventory.ItemMeta.has_display_name) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Checks for existence of a display name.

- [**has_repair_cost**](#endstone.inventory.ItemMeta.has_repair_cost) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Checks to see if this item has a repair penalty.
- [**is_unbreakable**](#endstone.inventory.ItemMeta.is_unbreakable) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Gets or sets the unbreakable tag. An unbreakable item will not lose durability.
- [**lore**](#endstone.inventory.ItemMeta.lore) (<code>[list](#list)\[[str](#str)\] | None</code>) – Gets or sets the lore for this item.

#### PlayerInventory [#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory]

Bases: <code>[Inventory](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Inventory)</code>

Interface to the inventory of a Player, including the four armor slots and any extra slots.

**Methods:**

- [**add_item**](#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory.add_item) – Stores the given ItemStacks in the inventory.
- [**get_item**](#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory.get_item) – Returns the ItemStack found in the slot at the given index
- [**remove_item**](#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory.remove_item) – Removes the given ItemStacks from the inventory.
- [**set_item**](#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory.set_item) – Stores the ItemStack at the given index of the inventory.

**Attributes:**

- [**boots**](#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory.boots) (<code>[ItemStack](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.ItemStack)</code>) – Gets or sets the ItemStack in the boots slot
- [**chestplate**](#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory.chestplate) (<code>[ItemStack](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.ItemStack)</code>) – Gets or sets the ItemStack in the chestplate slot
- [**contents**](#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory.contents) (<code>[list](#list)\[[ItemStack](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.ItemStack)\]</code>) – Returns all ItemStacks from the inventory
- [**first_empty**](#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory.first_empty) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Returns the first empty Slot.
- [**held_item_slot**](#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory.held_item_slot) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Gets or sets the slot number of the currently held item
- [**helmet**](#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory.helmet) (<code>[ItemStack](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.ItemStack)</code>) – Gets or sets the ItemStack in the helmet slot
- [**is_empty**](#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory.is_empty) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Check whether this inventory is empty. An inventory is considered to be empty if there are no ItemStacks in any slot of this inventory.
- [**item_in_main_hand**](#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory.item_in_main_hand) (<code>[ItemStack](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.ItemStack)</code>) – Gets or sets the item the player is currently holding in their main hand.
- [**item_in_off_hand**](#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory.item_in_off_hand) (<code>[ItemStack](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.ItemStack)</code>) – Gets or sets the item the player is currently holding in their off hand.
- [**leggings**](#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory.leggings) (<code>[ItemStack](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.ItemStack)</code>) – Gets or sets the ItemStack in the leg slot
- [**max_stack_size**](#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory.max_stack_size) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Returns the maximum stack size for an ItemStack in this inventory.
- [**size**](#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory.size) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Returns the size of the inventory

##### add_item [#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory.add_item]

```python
add_item(*args) -> dict[int, ItemStack]
```

Stores the given ItemStacks in the inventory.
This will try to fill existing stacks and empty slots as well as it can.

The returned map contains what it couldn't store, where the key is the index, and the value is the ItemStack.
If all items are stored, it will return an empty dict.

### map [#map]

**Classes:**

- [**MapCanvas**](#endstone.map.MapCanvas) – Represents a canvas for drawing to a map. Each canvas is associated with a specific MapRenderer and represents that renderer's layer on the map.
- [**MapRenderer**](#endstone.map.MapRenderer) – Represents a renderer for a map.
- [**MapView**](#endstone.map.MapView) – Represents a map item.

#### MapCanvas [#endstone.map.MapCanvas]

Represents a canvas for drawing to a map. Each canvas is associated with a specific MapRenderer and represents that renderer's layer on the map.

**Methods:**

- [**draw_image**](#endstone.map.MapCanvas.draw_image) – Draw an image to the map. The image will be clipped if necessary.
- [**get_base_pixel_color**](#endstone.map.MapCanvas.get_base_pixel_color) – Get a pixel from the layers below this canvas.
- [**get_pixel_color**](#endstone.map.MapCanvas.get_pixel_color) – Get a pixel from the canvas.
- [**set_pixel_color**](#endstone.map.MapCanvas.set_pixel_color) – Draw a pixel to the canvas.

**Attributes:**

- [**map_view**](#endstone.map.MapCanvas.map_view) (<code>[MapView](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.MapView)</code>) – Get the map this canvas is attached to.

##### draw_image [#endstone.map.MapCanvas.draw_image]

```python
draw_image(x:int, y:int, image:ndarray[uint8]) -> None
```

Draw an image to the map. The image will be clipped if necessary.

##### get_base_pixel_color [#endstone.map.MapCanvas.get_base_pixel_color]

```python
get_base_pixel_color(x:int, y:int) -> tuple[int, ...]
```

Get a pixel from the layers below this canvas.

##### get_pixel_color [#endstone.map.MapCanvas.get_pixel_color]

```python
get_pixel_color(x:int, y:int) -> tuple[int, ...] | None
```

Get a pixel from the canvas.

If no color is set at the given position for this canvas, then None is returned and the color returned by get_base_pixel_color() is shown on the map

##### map_view [#endstone.map.MapCanvas.map_view]

```python
map_view: MapView
```

Get the map this canvas is attached to.

##### set_pixel_color [#endstone.map.MapCanvas.set_pixel_color]

```python
set_pixel_color(x:int, y:int, color:tuple[int, ...] | None) -> None
```

Draw a pixel to the canvas.

If None is used as color, then the color returned by get_base_pixel_color() is shown on the map.

#### MapRenderer [#endstone.map.MapRenderer]

```python
MapRenderer(is_contextual:bool = False) -> None
```

Represents a renderer for a map.

**Methods:**

- [**initialize**](#endstone.map.MapRenderer.initialize) – Initialize this MapRenderer for the given map.
- [**render**](#endstone.map.MapRenderer.render) – Render to the given map.

Initialize the map renderer base with the given contextual status.


#### MapView [#endstone.map.MapView]

Represents a map item.

**Classes:**

- [**Scale**](#endstone.map.MapView.Scale) – An enum representing all possible scales a map can be set to.

**Methods:**

- [**add_renderer**](#endstone.map.MapView.add_renderer) – Add a renderer to this map.
- [**remove_renderer**](#endstone.map.MapView.remove_renderer) – Remove a renderer from this map.

**Attributes:**

- [**center_x**](#endstone.map.MapView.center_x) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Get or set the center X position of this map.
- [**center_z**](#endstone.map.MapView.center_z) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Get or set the center Z position of this map.
- [**dimension**](#endstone.map.MapView.dimension) (<code>[Dimension](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Dimension)</code>) – Get or set the dimension that this map is associated with.
- [**id**](#endstone.map.MapView.id) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Get the ID of this map item for use with MapMeta.
- [**is_unlimited_tracking**](#endstone.map.MapView.is_unlimited_tracking) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Whether the map will show a smaller position cursor (true), or no position cursor (false) when cursor is outside of map's range.
- [**is_virtual**](#endstone.map.MapView.is_virtual) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Check whether this map is virtual.
- [**locked**](#endstone.map.MapView.locked) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Whether the map is locked or not. A locked map may not be explored further.
- [**renderers**](#endstone.map.MapView.renderers) (<code>[list](#list)\[[MapRenderer](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.MapRenderer)\]</code>) – Get a copied list of MapRenderers currently in effect.
- [**scale**](#endstone.map.MapView.scale) (<code>[Scale](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.MapView.Scale)</code>) – Get or set the scale of this map.

### plugin [#plugin]

**Classes:**

- [**Plugin**](#endstone.plugin.Plugin) –
- [**PluginCommand**](#endstone.plugin.PluginCommand) – Represents a Command belonging to a Plugin
- [**PluginDescription**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription) – Represents the basic information about a plugin that the plugin loader needs to know.
- [**PluginLoadOrder**](#endstone.plugin.PluginLoadOrder) – Represents the order in which a plugin should be initialized and enabled.
- [**PluginLoader**](#endstone.plugin.PluginLoader) – Represents a plugin loader, which handles direct access to specific types of plugins
- [**PluginManager**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager) – Represents a plugin manager that handles all plugins from the Server
- [**Service**](#endstone.plugin.Service) – Represents a list of methods.
- [**ServiceManager**](#endstone.plugin.ServiceManager) – Represent a service manager that manages services and service providers.
- [**ServicePriority**](#endstone.plugin.ServicePriority) – Represents various priorities of a provider.

#### PluginCommand [#endstone.plugin.PluginCommand]

Bases: <code>[Command](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Command)</code>

Represents a Command belonging to a Plugin

**Methods:**

- [**execute**](#endstone.plugin.PluginCommand.execute) – Executes the command, returning its success
- [**test_permission**](#endstone.plugin.PluginCommand.test_permission) – Tests the given CommandSender to see if they can perform this command.
- [**test_permission_silently**](#endstone.plugin.PluginCommand.test_permission_silently) – Tests the given CommandSender to see if they can perform this command. No error is sent to the sender.

**Attributes:**

- [**aliases**](#endstone.plugin.PluginCommand.aliases) (<code>[list](#list)\[[str](#str)\]</code>) – List of aliases of this command
- [**description**](#endstone.plugin.PluginCommand.description) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Brief description of this command
- [**executor**](#endstone.plugin.PluginCommand.executor) (<code>[CommandExecutor](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.CommandExecutor)</code>) – The CommandExecutor to run when parsing this command
- [**is_registered**](#endstone.plugin.PluginCommand.is_registered) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns the current registered state of this command
- [**name**](#endstone.plugin.PluginCommand.name) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Name of this command.
- [**permissions**](#endstone.plugin.PluginCommand.permissions) (<code>[list](#list)\[[str](#str)\]</code>) – The permissions required by users to be able to perform this command
- [**plugin**](#endstone.plugin.PluginCommand.plugin) (<code>[Plugin](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Plugin)</code>) – The owner of this PluginCommand
- [**usages**](#endstone.plugin.PluginCommand.usages) (<code>[list](#list)\[[str](#str)\]</code>) – List of usages of this command

#### PluginDescription [#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription]

```python
PluginDescription(
    name: str,
    version: str,
    description: str | None = None,
    load: PluginLoadOrder | None = None,
    authors: list[str] | None = None,
    contributors: list[str] | None = None,
    website: str | None = None,
    prefix: str | None = None,
    provides: list[str] | None = None,
    depend: list[str] | None = None,
    soft_depend: list[str] | None = None,
    load_before: list[str] | None = None,
    default_permission: PermissionDefault | None = None,
    commands: list[Command] | None = None,
    permissions: list[Permission] | None = None,
    *args: list[Permission] | None,
    **kwargs: list[Permission] | None
) -> None
```

Represents the basic information about a plugin that the plugin loader needs to know.

**Attributes:**

- [**api_version**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription.api_version) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gives the API version which this plugin is designed to support.
- [**authors**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription.authors) (<code>[list](#list)\[[str](#str)\]</code>) – Gives the list of authors for the plugin.
- [**commands**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription.commands) (<code>[list](#list)\[[Command](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Command)\]</code>) – Gives the list of commands the plugin will register at runtime.
- [**contributors**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription.contributors) (<code>[list](#list)\[[str](#str)\]</code>) – Gives the list of contributors for the plugin.
- [**default_permission**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription.default_permission) (<code>[PermissionDefault](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.PermissionDefault)</code>) – Gives the default value of permissions registered for the plugin.
- [**depend**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription.depend) (<code>[list](#list)\[[str](#str)\]</code>) – Gives a list of other plugins that the plugin requires.
- [**description**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription.description) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gives a human-friendly description of the functionality the plugin provides.
- [**full_name**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription.full_name) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Returns the name of a plugin, including the version.
- [**load**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription.load) (<code>[PluginLoadOrder](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.PluginLoadOrder)</code>) – Gives the phase of server startup that the plugin should be loaded.
- [**load_before**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription.load_before) (<code>[list](#list)\[[str](#str)\]</code>) – Gets the list of plugins that should consider this plugin a soft-dependency.
- [**name**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription.name) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gives the name of the plugin. This name is a unique identifier for plugins.
- [**permissions**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription.permissions) (<code>[list](#list)\[[Permission](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Permission)\]</code>) – Gives the list of permissions the plugin will register at runtime, immediately proceeding enabling.
- [**prefix**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription.prefix) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gives the token to prefix plugin-specific logging messages with.
- [**provides**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription.provides) (<code>[list](#list)\[[str](#str)\]</code>) – Gives the list of other plugin APIs which this plugin provides. These are usable for other plugins to depend on.
- [**soft_depend**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription.soft_depend) (<code>[list](#list)\[[str](#str)\]</code>) – Gives a list of other plugins that the plugin requires for full functionality.
- [**version**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription.version) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gives the version of the plugin.
- [**website**](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription.website) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gives the plugin's or plugin's author's website.

#### PluginManager [#endstone.plugin.PluginManager]

Represents a plugin manager that handles all plugins from the Server

**Methods:**

- [**call_event**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.call_event) – Calls an event which will be passed to plugins.
- [**clear_plugins**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.clear_plugins) – Disables and removes all plugins
- [**disable_plugin**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.disable_plugin) – Disables the specified plugin
- [**disable_plugins**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.disable_plugins) – Disables all the loaded plugins
- [**enable_plugin**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.enable_plugin) – Enables the specified plugin
- [**enable_plugins**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.enable_plugins) – Enable all the loaded plugins
- [**get_default_perm_subscriptions**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.get_default_perm_subscriptions) – Gets a set containing all subscribed Permissibles to the given default list, by permission level.
- [**get_default_permissions**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.get_default_permissions) – Gets the default permissions for the given permission level.
- [**get_permission**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.get_permission) – Gets a Permission from its fully qualified name.
- [**get_permission_subscriptions**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.get_permission_subscriptions) – Gets a set containing all subscribed Permissibles to the given permission.
- [**get_plugin**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.get_plugin) – Checks if the given plugin is loaded and returns it when applicable.
- [**load_plugin**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.load_plugin) – Loads the plugin in the specified file
- [**recalculate_permission_defaults**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.recalculate_permission_defaults) – Recalculates the defaults for the given Permission.
- [**register_event**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.register_event) – Registers the given event
- [**subscribe_to_default_perms**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.subscribe_to_default_perms) – Subscribes to the given Default permissions by permission level.
- [**subscribe_to_permission**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.subscribe_to_permission) – Subscribes the given Permissible for information about the requested Permission.
- [**unsubscribe_from_default_perms**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.unsubscribe_from_default_perms) – Unsubscribes from the given Default permissions by permission level.
- [**unsubscribe_from_permission**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.unsubscribe_from_permission) – Unsubscribes the given Permissible for information about the requested Permission.

**Attributes:**

- [**permissions**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.permissions) (<code>[set](#set)\[[Permission](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Permission)\]</code>) – Gets a set of all registered permissions.
- [**plugins**](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.plugins) (<code>[list](#list)\[[Plugin](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Plugin)\]</code>) – Gets a list of all currently loaded plugins

##### call_event [#endstone.plugin.PluginManager.call_event]

### scheduler [#scheduler]

**Classes:**

- [**Scheduler**](#endstone.scheduler.Scheduler) – Represents a scheduler that executes various tasks
- [**Task**](#endstone.scheduler.Task) – Represents a task being executed by the scheduler

#### Scheduler [#endstone.scheduler.Scheduler]

Represents a scheduler that executes various tasks

**Methods:**

- [**cancel_task**](#endstone.scheduler.Scheduler.cancel_task) – Removes task from scheduler.
- [**cancel_tasks**](#endstone.scheduler.Scheduler.cancel_tasks) – Removes all tasks associated with a particular plugin from the scheduler.
- [**get_pending_tasks**](#endstone.scheduler.Scheduler.get_pending_tasks) – Returns a vector of all pending tasks.
- [**is_queued**](#endstone.scheduler.Scheduler.is_queued) – Check if the task queued to be run later.
- [**is_running**](#endstone.scheduler.Scheduler.is_running) – Check if the task currently running.
- [**run_task**](#endstone.scheduler.Scheduler.run_task) – Returns a task that will be executed synchronously

##### cancel_task [#endstone.scheduler.Scheduler.cancel_task]

```python
cancel_task(id:int) -> None
```

Removes task from scheduler.

##### cancel_tasks [#endstone.scheduler.Scheduler.cancel_tasks]

```python
cancel_tasks(plugin:Plugin) -> None
```

Removes all tasks associated with a particular plugin from the scheduler.

##### get_pending_tasks [#endstone.scheduler.Scheduler.get_pending_tasks]

```python
get_pending_tasks() -> list[Task]
```

Returns a vector of all pending tasks.

##### is_queued [#endstone.scheduler.Scheduler.is_queued]

```python
is_queued(id:int) -> bool
```

Check if the task queued to be run later.

##### is_running [#endstone.scheduler.Scheduler.is_running]

```python
is_running(id:int) -> bool
```

Check if the task currently running.

##### run_task [#endstone.scheduler.Scheduler.run_task]

```python
run_task(
    plugin: Plugin, task: Callable[[], None], delay: int = 0, period: int = 0
) -> Task
```

Returns a task that will be executed synchronously

#### Task [#endstone.scheduler.Task]

Represents a task being executed by the scheduler

**Methods:**

- [**cancel**](#endstone.scheduler.Task.cancel) – Attempts to cancel this task.

**Attributes:**

- [**is_cancelled**](#endstone.scheduler.Task.is_cancelled) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if the task has been cancelled.
- [**is_sync**](#endstone.scheduler.Task.is_sync) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Returns true if the task is run by server thread.
- [**owner**](#endstone.scheduler.Task.owner) (<code>[Plugin](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Plugin)</code>) – Returns the Plugin that owns the task.
- [**task_id**](#endstone.scheduler.Task.task_id) (<code>[int](#int)</code>) – Returns the task id.

##### cancel [#endstone.scheduler.Task.cancel]

```python
cancel() -> None
```

Attempts to cancel this task.

##### is_cancelled [#endstone.scheduler.Task.is_cancelled]

```python
is_cancelled: bool
```

Returns true if the task has been cancelled.

##### is_sync [#endstone.scheduler.Task.is_sync]

```python
is_sync: bool
```

Returns true if the task is run by server thread.

##### owner [#endstone.scheduler.Task.owner]

```python
owner: Plugin
```


#### Objective [#endstone.scoreboard.Objective]

Represents an objective on a scoreboard that can show scores specific to entries.

**Methods:**

- [**get_score**](#endstone.scoreboard.Objective.get_score) – Gets an entry's Score for this objective
- [**set_display**](#endstone.scoreboard.Objective.set_display) – Sets the display slot and sort order for this objective. This will remove it from any other display slot.
- [**unregister**](#endstone.scoreboard.Objective.unregister) – Unregisters this objective from the associated Scoreboard.

**Attributes:**

- [**criteria**](#endstone.scoreboard.Objective.criteria) (<code>[Criteria](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Criteria)</code>) – Gets the criteria this objective tracks
- [**display_name**](#endstone.scoreboard.Objective.display_name) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gets or sets the name displayed to players for this objective
- [**display_slot**](#endstone.scoreboard.Objective.display_slot) (<code>[DisplaySlot](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.DisplaySlot) | None</code>) – Gets or sets the display slot this objective is displayed at
- [**is_displayed**](#endstone.scoreboard.Objective.is_displayed) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Gets if the objective is currently displayed in a slot.
- [**is_modifiable**](#endstone.scoreboard.Objective.is_modifiable) (<code>[bool](#bool)</code>) – Gets if the objective's scores can be modified directly by a plugin
- [**name**](#endstone.scoreboard.Objective.name) (<code>[str](#str)</code>) – Gets the name of this Objective
- [**render_type**](#endstone.scoreboard.Objective.render_type) (<code>[RenderType](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.RenderType)</code>) – Gets the manner in which this objective will be rendered.
- [**scoreboard**](#endstone.scoreboard.Objective.scoreboard) (<code>[Scoreboard](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.Scoreboard)</code>) – Gets the scoreboard to which this objective is attached
- [**sort_order**](#endstone.scoreboard.Objective.sort_order) (<code>[ObjectiveSortOrder](#endstone._internal.endstone_python.ObjectiveSortOrder) | None</code>) – Gets or sets the sort order for this objective
